# #dot

## Basic Information
- Company: DotDot
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Smart Cities
- Categories: Smart Cities
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/dot/

![#dot](https://www.ces.tech/media/rf1beqce/dot.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
A #dot is a pocket-size WiFi hub to pair with the hotspot of one's smartphone to trade one's excess GB's anonymously on the #dotdot companion app. Sellers - named "#doter's" - purchase a #dot device to trade their excess GB's. Buyers - named "#dotee's" - just need to have a smartphone: even without existing internet access, #dotee's can connect to the "#dotdot" WiFi created by a nearby #doter, and purchase whatever quantity of GB's they need without subscription, just on demand.

# 10kM

## Basic Information
- Company: 10kM.ai
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Mobile Devices, Accessories & Apps
- Categories: Mobile Devices, Accessories & Apps
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/10km/

![10kM](https://www.ces.tech/media/hyzekzmr/10km.jpg?rxy=0.46994969491450284,0.5045445887460003&width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
10kM is a mobile app that helps individuals and businesses transform text-based documents into fully editable, professional-grade videos in just one minute. It analyzes document structures and reference videos to automatically generate video formats with CSS animations, all of which can be edited in real time. Designed for those with minimal video editing skills, 10kM significantly reduces the time and cost of video production, making it easy to create high-quality digital content.

# 3D SPATIAL MAPPING KEYSTONE CORRECTION

## Basic Information
- Company: Samsung Electronics America, Inc.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Mobile Devices, Accessories & Apps
- Categories: Mobile Devices, Accessories & Apps
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/3d-spatial-mapping-keystone-correction/

![3D SPATIAL MAPPING KEYSTONE CORRECTION](https://www.ces.tech/media/vahbydv1/3dspatialmappingkeystonecorrection.png?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Ultra short-throw projectors can make any space the ultimate home entertainment setup. However, most require manual calibration to display clear, squared-off images. This cumbersome process often calls for professional support, and all it takes is mistakenly bumping the projector to throw it off.Samsung 3D Spatial Mapping Keystone Correction bypasses challenging calibration. You simply take a picture of a calibration image in the SmartThings app. The projector does the rest—in under a second.People get projectors for their cinematic experience. This feature powers exactly that, while eliminating time-consuming setup, so your next movie night is just a tap away.

# 3D Visualization of a X-ray image & Visibility Enhancement

## Basic Information
- Company: Korea Institute of Science and Technology
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Artificial Intelligence
- Categories: Artificial Intelligence
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/3d-visualization-of-a-x-ray-image-visibility-enhancement/

![3D Visualization of a X-ray image & Visibility Enhancement](https://www.ces.tech/media/12yfzpvr/3dvisualizationofax-rayimagevisibilityenhancement.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
This product leverages advanced deep learning to perform two key functions: transforming a 2D single shot X-ray image into high-resolution 3D visualizations and enhancing visibility in adverse weather conditions such as fog, rain, snow, sandstorm, smoke from fires and underwater environments. The 3D X-ray image transforming technology has significant applications in healthcare diagnosis for some hospitals without CT (Computed Tomography) or similar detectors. Visibility improvement technology enhances image clarity in diverse weather situations, allowing for quicker response and life-saving interventions, thereby supporting accident prevention. These two technologies ultimately target humanitarian efforts.

# AgriShield

## Basic Information

## Description

To address this, HL Klemove has developed AgriShield, a high-performance wildlife deterrent equipped with robust sensors and AI. AgriShield is built to be durable, highly effective and capable of recognizing different animals. It keeps farmlands safe by detecting and deterring animals, using customized methods for each species.

# Ailive Studio

## Basic Information
- Company: Ailive Inc.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Artificial Intelligence
- Categories: Artificial Intelligence
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/ailive-studio/

![Ailive Studio](https://www.ces.tech/media/1mmp0rcb/ailivestudio.jpg?rxy=0.5025039384227484,0.5071488833499453&width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Ailive Studio is an innovative web service that leverages AI technology to enable anyone, even without knowledge of 3D production, to easily create high-quality 3D content. Ailive Studio uses Image to 3D AI technology to automatically generate rigged 3D characters, employs LLM to analyze the story and scripts, and recommends backgrounds and characters. It also utilizes Text to Motion and Text to Speech AI to create character motions and dialogue. By offering these synergistic AI technologies in an easy-to-use format, Ailive Studio allows users to turn their ideas into 3D animations in just a few minutes with simple operations.

# Aiper IrriSense Smart Irrigation System

## Basic Information
- Company: Aiper Intelligent, LLC
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Home Appliances
- Categories: Home Appliances
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/aiper-irrisense-smart-irrigation-system/

![Aiper IrriSense Smart Irrigation System](https://www.ces.tech/media/pjjjt1ly/aiperirrisensesmartirrigationsystem.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The Aiper IrriSense Smart Irrigation System revolutionizes lawn care by simulating natural rainfall for optimal hydration. Designed for areas up to 400 square meters, it features a customizable mapping function, allowing users to set specific spray points and reduce water usage by up to 50%. The innovative Re-Spray Algorithm ensures 99% coverage, automatically targeting under-watered sections for even growth. Users can also adjust watering schedules based on real-time weather data and soil conditions, ensuring efficient irrigation. The Plant Cooling Mode offers quick bursts of irrigation through the Aiper App, cooling the lawn on hot days without oversaturation. Installation takes just three minutes, with no underground piping needed, making it user-friendly. The system also stores and dispenses fertilizers and pesticides at the push of a button. Its compact design seamlessly integrates into any backyard, enhancing the overall ecosystem. In summary, the Aiper IrriSense is a cutting-edge solution that minimizes water waste while ensuring healthy, lush lawns.

# AirJet Mini Sport

## Basic Information
- Company: Frore Systems
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Computer Hardware & Components
- Categories: Computer Hardware & Components
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/airjet-mini-sport/

![AirJet Mini Sport](https://www.ces.tech/media/v43b5l4e/airjetminisport.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
AirJet® Mini Sport, by Frore Systems, the world’s first IP68 compliant solid-state active cooling chip, is designed to unleash performance in waterproof IP68 Devices. The chip is a breakthrough in consumer device heat removal that enables the full potential of IP68 devices like smartphones, action cameras and even SSD accessories to be realized. Embedding one or multiple AirJet chips in IP68 consumer products enables active heat removal which solves the thermal issues causing device performance to throttle. The award-winning AirJet Mini Sport has demonstrated record-breaking improvements of up to 3x in performance across a wide range of applications.

# AirShifter

## Basic Information
- Company: Proxgy
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Home Appliances
- Categories: Home Appliances
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/airshifter/

![AirShifter](https://www.ces.tech/media/nrzffkkt/airshifter.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
AirShifter is a smart ceiling fan that intelligently adapts to your room's needs. Equipped with a built-in LiDAR sensor, it automatically adjusts airflow based on room size and layout, while its rotatable pitch angle ensures optimal air distribution. AirShifter also features an integrated HEPA purifier and UV light, delivering clean, purified air as it cools. In larger spaces, multiple AirShifter fans can communicate with each other to harmonize airflow, providing a seamless and comfortable environment throughout the room.

# AI Echo Care

## Basic Information
- Company: Inviz Corporation
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Artificial Intelligence
- Categories: Artificial Intelligence
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/ai-echo-care/

![AI Echo Care](https://www.ces.tech/media/xizhxhgo/aiechocare.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
AI Echo Care, developed by Inviz, utilizes artificial intelligence technology to transform the traditionally complex and time-consuming echocardiography process. By automating key aspects and enhancing diagnostic precision, our technology enables the completion of over 10 heart examinations per hour, compared to the previous maximum of 3. This significant improvement not only optimizes physicians' time and examination accuracy but also reduces patient fatigue caused by prolonged wait times. Furthermore, AI Echo Care significantly lowers the risk of misdiagnosis by achieving a 93% accuracy rate in detecting heart diseases, making it a critical tool in modern cardiac care.

# All Lenses on Prism (ALoP)

## Basic Information
- Company: Samsung Electronics America, Inc.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Imaging
- Categories: Imaging
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/all-lenses-on-prism-alop/

![All Lenses on Prism (ALoP)](https://www.ces.tech/media/op4clyvk/alllensesonprism.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Samsung’s ALoP is a next generation telephoto camera solution with new folded zoom structure. Unlike the conventional model, it places the lenses directly on the prism rather than in-between prism and sensor. With such new structural improvement, ALoP is able to improve brightness and reduce noise while decreasing the module shoulder height and length.The shoulder height and length of the module can be directly translated to amount of camera bump, which has been the pain point for smartphone designers. With ALoP, the reduced module shoulder height and length will allow more aesthetic design, benefiting both users and device developers.


---

# AMD Ryzen 7 9800X3D

## Basic Information
- Company: Advanced Micro Devices, Inc.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Computer Hardware & Components
- Categories: Computer Hardware & Components
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/amd-ryzen-7-9800x3d/

![AMD Ryzen 7 9800X3D](https://www.ces.tech/media/ww4nh5ad/amdryzen79800x3d.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Combined with the advanced "Zen 5" processor architecture, the AMD 3D V-Cache technology works to attain the highest processor gaming performance on the market. Ryzen 7 9800X3D processor can demonstrate substantial generational improvements in minimum frame rates even when average frame rates are similar, providing the user with an experience that feels smoother, with less stutter. With the AMD Ryzen 7 9800X3D processor, AMD has re-engineered its cutting-edge on-chip memory solution with 2nd Gen AMD 3D V-Cache technology. The 64MB cache memory has been relocated below the processor, which puts the core complex die (CCD) closer to the cooling solution to help keep the "Zen 5" cores cooler, delivering high clock rates and providing up to an average 8% gaming performance improvement compared to the last-generation Ryzen X3D and up to an average 20% faster than the competition. This revolutionary change in placement allows for extreme overclocking of the processor. It's the first X3D processor to be fully unlocked, empowering enthusiasts and gamers to push its performance to new limits.

- Company: Anker Innovations Ltd

- Categories: Computer Peripherals & Accessories
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/anker-prime-charging-docking-station-14-in-1-160w/

![Anker Prime Charging Docking Station (14-in-1, 160W）](https://www.ces.tech/media/zj3iilo0/anker-prime-charging-docking-station.png?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Anker Prime 14-in-1 Charging Docking Station provides 160W fast charging via 4 ports (USB-C3, USB-A1), dual 4K displays through 2 HDMI ports, and ultra-fast data transfer with 2 USB-C and 1 USB-A port (10Gbps). It also includes 1 Ethernet port, 1 audio output, and 3 USB ports with 480Mbps transfer speeds. The smart screen display offers real-time status updates, while the integrated GaN power module and vertical design reduce clutter, making it ideal for efficient, multi-device connectivity in compact spaces.

# ArthronPulse

## Basic Information
- Company: EntWick Inc.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Digital Health
- Categories: Digital Health
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/arthronpulse/

![ArthronPulse](https://www.ces.tech/media/kp1afco4/arthronpulse.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
ArthronPulse is a personal electronic therapy device for degenerative arthritis that applies non-invasive treatments using pulsed electromagnetic fields therapy(PEMFt), low-level laser therapy (LLLt), and electrical muscle stimulation (EMS).The PEMFt suppress the expression of inflammation-inducing factors in arthritis, while the LLLt provides pain relief, and the EMS promotes joint health by strengthening the muscles.This wearable electronic device maximizes therapeutic effects by incorporating various non-invasive treatment technologies, and it also features built-in wireless network technology, enabling remote treatment with doctors for personal digital healthcare.

# ARTIS (AR Training for Intervention & Surgery)

## Basic Information
- Company: Decasight Corp.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Digital Health
- Categories: Digital Health
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/artis-ar-training-for-intervention-surgery/

![ARTIS (AR Training for Intervention & Surgery)](https://www.ces.tech/media/p1ye3lh3/014306b2-5b50-470c-979f-01a216e75229.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
ARTIS is the world’s first AR training simulator for invasive clinical procedures and surgical training. ARTIS consists of three modes: Learning, Training, and Testing. In Learning Mode, ARTIS provides background medical knowledges on a variety of essential invasive procedures, including target patients, methods, and precautions. In Training Mode, learners can perform procedures on elaborately crafted silicone models that resemble actual anatomical structures, allowing them to repeatedly train in the most effective and safe procedures. Finally, in Testing Mode, entire procedures can be performed sequentially without AR guidance and clinical appropriateness is assessed by a score and communicated to educators.

# A laser-induced thrombosis on a chip

## Basic Information
- Company: Taiwan Tech Arena
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Beauty & Personal Care
- Categories: Beauty & Personal Care
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/a-laser-induced-thrombosis-on-a-chip/

![A laser-induced thrombosis on a chip](https://www.ces.tech/media/sz2dehpz/alaser-inducedthrombosisonachip.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The laser-induced thrombosis-on-a-Chip is an integrated system that mimics blood clot  in vitro for multifunctional testing platform. It combines microfluidic systems, tissue culture, and photoinduction to create a localized thrombus model. This platform enables visualized thrombus modeling across species, drug testing for thrombosis prevention. Different from other thrombosis-on-a-chip devices, using chemical to induce endothelium inflammation, our unique part is using laser to locally treat  endothelium inflammation. We can generate thrombus in a specific location (with laser illumination) in a microfluidic channel.

# buddy-in

## Basic Information
- Company: Neudive Inc
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Digital Health
- Categories: Digital Health
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/buddy-in/

![buddy-in](https://www.ces.tech/media/zcad5mrg/101322327_new_image_buddy-in_1913043.png?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
‘buddy-in’ is a cutting-edge digital therapeutics designed for children and adolescents with Autism Spectrum Disorder (ASD) and Social Communication Disorder (SCD) through Digital Social Skills Training. Delivered as a social simulation game set in a school environment, it offers engaging and interactive practice by adapting to each user's progress to tailor the learning experience. Children and adolescents can use ‘buddy-in’ independently on their mobile phones and practice with caregivers to perform real-world activities that help generalize the skills learned in digital therapeutic. The gamified design enhances user engagement and adherence to the program. With its simple structure—just 15 minutes per day, five times a week for six weeks—‘buddy-in’ fits seamlessly into home-based routines. In a randomized, controlled pilot clinical trial, the initial safety and efficacy were statistically demonstrated. Currently, a confirmatory clinical trial is underway, aiming for approval from the Korean Ministry of Food and Drug Safety (MFDS) in 2025.

# CARELINK

## Description
The plasma endodontic treatment device treats infected tooth pulp, easing pain and swelling by removing damaged tissue and filling the space. It creates plasma discharge between two separate electrodes, using tiny currents to clear inflamed material, disinfect, and stop bleeding in the root canal. The device manages power well by changing the gap and voltage of electrodes to avoid excess current. It also has an LED display that shows energy strength through colors, letting users easily check and set the power level.

# CART VITAL (project 'Apollon')

## Basic Information
- Company: Sky Labs
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Artificial Intelligence
- Categories: Artificial Intelligence
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/cart-vital-project-apollon/

![CART VITAL (project 'Apollon')](https://www.ces.tech/media/2xdpnwmb/101322327_apollon_ces_logo.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
'CART VITAL' (project name, Apollon) is a pioneering wearable designed for comprehensive monitoring of vital health indicators. Integrating both a wrist-worn module and a ring-type sensor, CART VITAL automatically and periodically measures SpO₂, irregular pulse, pulse rate, blood pressure, respiration rate, and skin temperature, while also offering on-demand body temperature measurements. Engineered with hospitalized patients in mind, Apollon supports extensive tracking of health data, providing valuable insights for health monitoring and treatment.CART VITAL is a device developed in collaboration between Sky Labs and Ilsan Hospital of the NHIS (National Health Insurance Service) for the purpose of carrying out a project for the MoHW (Ministry of Health and Welfare).

- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Vehicle Tech & Advanced Mobility
- Categories: Vehicle Tech & Advanced Mobility
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/cryoflux-powercable/

## Description
CryoFlux PowerCableThe liquid evaporation phase change Ultra-Fast Charging Cable is the world’s first lightweight, high-efficiency charging solution using liquid phase change cooling to address weight and overheating issues in megawatt charging.As fast-charging technology advances, cables become thicker and heavier, leading to overheating and safety concerns, especially for large electric vehicles, ships, and UAM systems.Our cable’s cold zone, reaching below -40°C, prevents overheating, enabling safe, efficient current transmission at a weight under 10 kg, with over 50% higher efficiency.We offer a reliable, lightweight megawatt-level charging solution, advancing electric mobility adoption.

# CXL-Based GPU Memory Expansion Kit

## Basic Information
- Company: Panmnesia, Inc.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Computer Peripherals & Accessories
- Categories: Computer Peripherals & Accessories
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/cxl-based-gpu-memory-expansion-kit/

![CXL-Based GPU Memory Expansion Kit](https://www.ces.tech/media/s4vdkmke/cxl-basedgpumemoryexpansionkit.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Panmnesia’s CXL-Based GPU Memory Expansion Kit eliminates the GPU memory capacity limitations with innovative Compute eXpress Link (CXL) technology for large AI models such as LLMs and GenAI. The CXL empowers the GPU to enjoy terabytes of memory space by connecting it to multiple memory expanders through the CXL network. Such ample memory resources allow AI service providers to run large AI models with 34 times less system CAPEX. In addition, our kit employs Panmnesia’s optimized CXL controller that exhibits the world’s first two-digit nanosecond latency, offering high speed for memory expansion.

# DEBREX

## Basic Information
- Company: FUST Lab. Co., Ltd.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Industrial Equipment and Machinery
- Categories: Industrial Equipment and Machinery
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/debrex/

![DEBREX](https://www.ces.tech/media/rdgf0lvn/4480057c-bdb6-4463-bc89-c637039748d0.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
FUST Lab's ultrasonic emulsification/dispersion device is a world’s first manufacturing equipment that uniformly mixes immiscible substances (like water, oil) together to produce functional materials in uniform nanoscale without surfactants. This advancement enhances the incorporation of active ingredients and improves particle performance without compromising functionality. Traditionally, surfactants have been added to the mixture due to technological limitation, despite its negative impact on performance, health, and environment. This technology will enhance the quality and performance of the products in the fields of pharmaceuticals, cosmetics, batteries, coatings, and food production, thus contributing positively to an elevated quality of life.

## Description

# DisMantleBot: Modular Robots for Dismantling EV Battery

## Basic Information
- Company: THOTH.Inc
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Sustainability & Energy/Power, Robotics, Human Security for All
- Categories: Sustainability & Energy/Power, Robotics, Human Security for All
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/dismantlebot-modular-robots-for-dismantling-ev-battery/

![DisMantleBot: Modular Robots for Dismantling EV Battery](https://www.ces.tech/media/m4wljmar/dismantlebotmodularrobotsfordismantlingevbattery.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
DisMantleBot is a cutting-edge modular robotic system designed for the efficient and precise dismantling of Electric Vehicle (EV) batteries. DisMantleBot determines the optimal disassembly level—complete or partial—based on battery grades and selects the appropriate disassembly methods, such as separation and cutting. The system systematically disassembles battery packs into modules, modules into cells, and cells into components like anodes, cathodes, and separators. Additionally, DisMantleBot carefully disassembles all related components—battery covers, wires, hoses, connectors, cushioning materials, bolts, and nuts—ensuring a thorough and meticulous dismantling process. Users customize and deploy multiple units according to their specific needs and quantities.

# EB corbos Linux for Safety Applications

- Company: Elektrobit
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Vehicle Tech & Advanced Mobility
- Categories: Vehicle Tech & Advanced Mobility
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/eb-corbos-linux-for-safety-applications/

## Description
EB corbos Linux for Safety Applications is the world’s first open-source-based automotive operating system (OS) solution for safety-relevant applications to receive a positive assessment for certification by the global organization, TÜV Nord. Long the norm in other industries, the impact of free, open-source software in automotive has been limited by the industry’s strict safety requirements. This innovative solution allows carmakers to use Linux for applications such as ADAS and autonomous driving. It paves the way for the development of safer and more reliable vehicles, accelerating the transition towards the software-defined vehicle (SDV), also called the smart car of the future.

# Efficient E1

## Basic Information
- Company: Efficient Computer
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Computer Hardware & Components
- Categories: Computer Hardware & Components
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/efficient-e1/

![Efficient E1](https://www.ces.tech/media/4imcdzoo/ebc53638-b4f5-4b98-9ffb-da460184b593.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Efficient introduces a new category of general-purpose computer processor, up to 100x more energy-efficient than leading, low-power CPUs on the market. Efficient’s Fabric architecture, a unique approach to general-purpose computation, eliminates energy overheads of general-purpose “von-Neumann” architectures. Class-defining energy efficiency enables battery-powered devices to last years, not weeks, and supports expanded on-device computing capabilities at the edge. The Fabric makes application development fast and easy, with developer-friendly support of mainstream and high-level programming languages and application frameworks (e.g., AI). Building on a decade of world-class research at Carnegie Mellon, Efficient is disrupting the space and driving unprecedented general-purpose computing efficiency.

# Ethereal (Digital Twin 3D Modelling Solution)

## Basic Information
- Company: Ethereal 
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Industrial Equipment and Machinery
- Categories: Industrial Equipment and Machinery
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/ethereal-digital-twin-3d-modelling-solution/

![Ethereal (Digital Twin 3D Modelling Solution)](https://www.ces.tech/media/tphpbrc1/101322327_ethereal_image010.png?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Ethereal suggests a new paradigm of intuitive 3D modelling through a physical digital-twin interface. 3D data can be created as a real-time synced digital twin, directly formed and modified via user input on the physical build plate. The 45x45 array of modular pins that compose the build plate are controlled via a microcontroller and a series of linear actuators to mimic parts of the 3D model's surface. Panning, rotating and zooming the digital twin model through the embedded touch screen in reorientation mode, users can also update the model surface displayed on the screen onto the build plate.

# Farady Reactor

## Basic Information
- Company: VVater
- Honor: 2025 Best of Innovation in Sustainability & Energy/Power
- Categories: Sustainability & Energy/Power
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/farady-reactor/

![Farady Reactor](https://www.ces.tech/media/xruby2pr/faradyreactor.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The Faraday Reactor is an innovative water treatment technology designed to provide efficient and chemical-free purification of various water sources, including wastewater. This cutting-edge reactor uses the Advanced Low Tension Electroporation Process (A.L.T.E.P.) to break down contaminants, such as unwanted microorganisms and organic pollutants, without the need for additional chemicals, filters, membranes, or biological agents. The Farady Reactors also generate hydroxyl radicals, thus eliminating the need for chemical residue. The Farady Reactor has been named a revelation in the industry and classified as one of the planet's most advanced water treatment machines.

# Feed Heat Monitor® - first ever wearable cow health monitor

## Basic Information
- Company: HRG Inc.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Pet Tech & Animal Welfare
- Categories: Pet Tech & Animal Welfare
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/feed-heat-monitor-first-ever-wearable-cow-health-monitor/

![Feed Heat Monitor® - first ever wearable cow health monitor](https://www.ces.tech/media/dm4pddlu/48f6c751-1755-4213-af15-b4ab00ac0632.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The first-ever wearable device for cows, designed to maximize production output with enhanced efficiency, monitors eight vital signals: heart rate, respiration, feed intake (RFI), rumination, estrus, activity levels, lameness, and weight gain. This easy-latch device addresses the growing challenges of large-scale farming by providing early detection of infections and optimizing farm management. It also supports national disease control efforts and enables feed companies to enhance brand loyalty and sales by bundling this advanced technology with their products.

# FingerVision R1

## Basic Information
- Company: FingerVision
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Robotics
- Categories: Robotics
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/fingervision-r1/

![FingerVision R1](https://www.ces.tech/media/z2yhjynn/eb395f9d-3d08-43e7-995d-5f032051f350.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
FingerVision R1 marks a revolutionary leap in industrial robotics as the world's first implementation of tactile sensors, utilizing cutting-edge optical tactile sensing technology for enhanced object manipulation. This groundbreaking development allows FingerVision R1 to automate complex tasks such as accurately placing varied and irregularly shaped food items on bento assembly lines-previously deemed unachievable. This achievement introduces the first-ever commercial use of a robot capable of directly handling food ingredients, setting a new standard in the food industry. This product can be implemented in various industries including automobiles, electrical equipment, materials, semiconductors, logistics, and medical care.

# FRENZ FocusFlow

## Basic Information
- Company: Earable Neuroscience
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Digital Health
- Categories: Digital Health
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/frenz-focusflow/

![FRENZ FocusFlow](https://www.ces.tech/media/jielhgcu/59e385e8-57e5-4e1a-bdd2-7e943f1d82d7.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
FRENZ FocusFlow combines real-time brain signal tracking with personalized audio therapy to enhance cognitive clarity and promote mental well-being. Over 50% of the world population struggles with maintaining focus throughout the day. FRENZ FocusFlow app offers 24/7 biomarker monitoring for mental health and cognitive performance. FocusFlow’s patented algorithms deliver science-backed interventions based on EEG neurofeedback, helping users maintain focus and mental stability. Key features include continuous focus tracking, personalized cognitive therapy, and an open content library for therapists. Real-world trials show a 70% improvement in focus over 30 days, making FocusFlow a breakthrough digital health platform for mental well-being.

- Company: SGLAB Inc.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Fitness

- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/g-grip-worlds-first-ai-powered-intelligent-golf-club/

## Description

Golfers struggle with maintaining proper grip pressure and consistent swing paths, critical for performance and injury prevention. G-Grip provides instant, coach-like feedback, optimizing grip and swing, transforming every stroke into a data-driven performance moment. By revealing previously invisible insights, G-Grip empowers you to build better habits and elevate your game. From tee to green, it unlocks your potential, revolutionizing how you play and improve.

# Gait Beauty Measurement System

## Basic Information
- Company: Shiseido Co., Ltd.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Beauty & Personal Care
- Categories: Beauty & Personal Care
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/gait-beauty-measurement-system/

![Gait Beauty Measurement System](https://www.ces.tech/media/tnngt4x5/gaitbeautymeasurementsystem.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
"Gait" refers to the posture, stride and arm swing that a person has when walking, and it has a significant impact on the impression that one makes on others. This new experience we have created focuses on how one's gait can make a beautiful impression by visualizing the invisible impressions that we make. Based on the results, personalized recommendations can be provided to help people achieve their ideal gait. Maintaining a beautiful gait improves the beauty of one's movements and gestures while changing the body from the inside out, improving how one's face is perceived as well.

# GenGenStudio: GenAI based synthetic data production S/W

## Basic Information
- Company: GenGenAI
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Artificial Intelligence
- Categories: Artificial Intelligence
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/gengenstudio-genai-based-synthetic-data-production-sw/

![GenGenStudio: GenAI based synthetic data production S/W](https://www.ces.tech/media/coeb3sew/8c1a0460-0271-49f3-b70e-21369588008b.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
GenGenStudio is a synthetic data generation software platform using domain-specific generative AI to create high-quality images and videos for AI training. It serves industries like automotive, providing data without manual collection. The platform simulates various driving conditions and generates data for rare scenarios, such as animals or accidents, seasons and weathers, which are hard to capture manually. It also produces diverse driver images for monitoring systems. By automating data generation, GenGenStudio reduces costs and development time, enhancing AI accuracy and safety. This makes AI development more efficient and affordable for mobility related companies (e.g., Ford, GM, Magna, etc.).

## Description

# H-Medi: All-in-one Gait Rehabilitation and Prognosis

## Basic Information
- Company: Hurotics Inc.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Accessibility & AgeTech, Robotics
- Categories: Accessibility & AgeTech, Robotics
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/h-medi-all-in-one-gait-rehabilitation-and-prognosis/

![H-Medi: All-in-one Gait Rehabilitation and Prognosis](https://www.ces.tech/media/k1xhmh2c/05dd6e34-90fa-4aa1-8c33-496b82d7fdf9.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
H-Medi is the world’s first advanced all-in-one wearable medical robot for gait disorders, seamlessly integrating the full-cycle rehabilitation process. With AI capable of predicting disease prognosis with 92% accuracy, H-Medi refines treatment by analyzing individual gait patterns, leading to over a 10% improvement in walking speed. Its on-device AI delivers customized support within 2 minutes, using adaptive algorithms to assess and assist with 95% accuracy, enhancing gait efficiency by up to 21%. This comprehensive approach ensures precise, personalized rehabilitation, effectively addressing the growing challenge of gait disorders in a super-aged society, while fostering a healthier lifestyle for elderly patients.

# HISONG SuperMic S1

## Basic Information
- Company: Hisong Music Technology Inc.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Audio Video Components & Accessories
- Categories: Audio Video Components & Accessories
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/hisong-supermic-s1/

![HISONG SuperMic S1](https://www.ces.tech/media/bwwburjb/hisong-supermic-s1-part-2.png?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
HISONG 3-in-1 SuperMic S1The S1 offers a groundbreaking, truly wireless, and portable audio workstation. Leveraging highly innovative and patented wireless audio technologies, it seamlessly integrates three essential functions—microphone, audio mixer, and earphones—into a single solution. This integration enhances both efficiency and convenience, representing a major advancement in the audio industry.The microphone features proprietary acoustic structures and algorithms, enabling effortless switching among multi-directional pickup patterns (cardioid, supercardioid, etc.) via a distributed microphone system.The built-in audio mixer is equipped with a powerful DSP (Digital Signal Processor) for complex floating-point calculations.The monitoring earphones utilize the latest LE AUDIO wireless technology.Furthermore, when paired with the HISONG LINK app, the S1 provides professional-grade vocal fine-tuning capabilities with a built-in EQ (Equalizer).With its exceptional hardware and software solution, the HISONG S1 delivers truly one-of-a-kind performance for live streaming, recording, music creation, or everyday listening and singing.

# HL HAECHIE

## Basic Information
- Company: HL Mando
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Human Security for All
- Categories: Human Security for All
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/hl-haechie/

![HL HAECHIE](https://www.ces.tech/media/2trlmk4i/7e18d982-d140-4ffa-9821-cd8875bda13d.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
HL HAECHIE is an innovative device that detects ultraviolet radiation emitted during arc occurrences, which are a primary cause of electrical fires. By accurately sensing UV-C with advanced semiconductor technology, it enables electrical fires to be detected early and prevented without malfunctions. HL HAECHIE's wide detection range, compact size, and easy installation mean it can be applied to both small electronic devices and large electrical systems. In an increasingly electrified world, it introduces a new paradigm in fire prevention, providing a safer environment.

# Holographic Extended Reality (HXR) platform

## Basic Information
- Company: Swave Photonics
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in XR Technologies & Accessories
- Categories: XR Technologies & Accessories
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/holographic-extended-reality-hxr-platform/

![Holographic Extended Reality (HXR) platform](https://www.ces.tech/media/ytyaqv2y/holographicextendedreality-hxr-platform.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Swave’s Holographic eXtended Reality (HXR) is the world’s first true holographic display technology that sculpts and steers light to form high-resolution 3D images. HXR establishes a new kind of advanced display technology, producing the world’s smallest pixel with a pixel pitch of less than 300nm. The low-cost CMOS chip technology will enable AI-powered spatial computing for compact smart glasses and other XR form factors. The technology will provide a reality-first user experience, where digital elements complement, learn from, and interact with the physical world. Use cases will be vast, including healthcare, manufacturing, logistics, retail, communication, gaming, education, automotive and aerospace.

## Description

# HyperGrid NX

## Basic Information
- Company: LS ELECTRIC Co., Ltd., LS Cable & System Ltd.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Human Security for All, Smart Cities
- Categories: Human Security for All, Smart Cities
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/hypergrid-nx/

![HyperGrid NX](https://www.ces.tech/media/yo5hydsk/hypergrid-nx.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The HyperGrid NX is a superconducting power system that sets a new standard for next-generation power delivery, offering high-capacity transmission with improved reliability and protection. This was jointly developed by LS ELECTRIC Co., Ltd. and LS Cable & System Ltd.. The HyperGrid NX is an optimal solution for large power consumers, such as urban data centers and advanced industrial complexes. It minimizes the need for power grid expansion and construction, reducing both construction time and costs, while preventing damage from power outages or fires. Furthermore, there are no electromagnetic wave emissions and transmission losses during power transmission, enhancing the acceptance of transmission and transformation facilities in densely populated urban areas and contributing to carbon emission reduction.

# IMMERSIO™ XE50 Battery System

## Basic Information
- Company: XING Mobility
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Sustainability & Energy/Power
- Categories: Sustainability & Energy/Power
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/immersio-xe50-battery-system/

![IMMERSIO™ XE50 Battery System](https://www.ces.tech/media/u4paxqth/immersioxe50batterysystem.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Designed for energy storage system, the IMMERSIO™ XE50 Battery System revolutionizes battery performance by immersing cells in dielectric fluid for coolant for efficient cooling. With precise temperature control within 3% and an innovative structural design, the system extends battery life by 15% and saves approximately 40% in space and weight, thereby reducing operational costs. Additionally, it overcomes the safety and temperature limitations of lithium batteries, enabling energy storage system deployment from urban environments to extreme climates, and accelerating the energy transition.

# IM_Pathfinder_Navi

## Basic Information
- Company: IMSYSTEM Co., Ltd.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Robotics
- Categories: Robotics
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/im_pathfinder_navi/

![IM_Pathfinder_Navi](https://www.ces.tech/media/z1gpquxr/im_pathfinder_navi.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
IM_Pathfinder_Navi is a next-generation robotic intervention system designed to treat critical vascular diseases such as thrombosis, myocardial infarction, and stroke - among the leading causes of global mortality. This innovative system provides easy, fast, and precise 3D steering of magnetic guidewires through its advanced magnetic field control, significantly reducing procedure time. Shorter procedures not only minimize patient radiation exposure but also enable quicker recovery. Medical staff can operate the system remotely using controls like a 3D mouse or joystick, allowing them to perform surgeries from a separate area and reducing their radiation exposure to nearly zero.

# In-Mold Structural Electronics (IMSE®)

## Basic Information
- Company: TactoTek
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Vehicle Tech & Advanced Mobility
- Categories: Vehicle Tech & Advanced Mobility
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/in-mold-structural-electronics-imse/

![In-Mold Structural Electronics (IMSE®)](https://www.ces.tech/media/m0pbb1dy/in-moldstructuralelectronics-imse.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
In-mold structural electronics (IMSE®) is a technology platform that integrates electronics, mechanics and cosmetics within a single-piece, seamless, 3D injection molded part. IMSE parts re light weight, thin, and durable, they also reduce complexity by replacing multi-part conventional electronics assemblies. Circuitry, touch controls, proximity sensors, antennas, and lighting are common features in IMSE designs. Surface treatments include cosmetic plastics and natural materials, including wood veneer. Even with integrated lighting, IMSE parts can be as thin as 3mm and conform to complex shapes supporting unprecedented design freedom for incorporating electronic features in vehicle interiors and exteriors.

# Intelligent Illuminated Door Panel

## Basic Information
- Company: TactoTek
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Vehicle Tech & Advanced Mobility
- Categories: Vehicle Tech & Advanced Mobility
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/intelligent-illuminated-door-panel/

## Description
TactoTek's Intelligent Illuminated Door Panel uses patented Surface Light™ technology for edge-to-edge dynamic lighting that maximizes uniformity and minimizes the number of LEDs in ultra-thin packaging. Surface Light outperforms traditional PCBA electronics and OLEDs, and is suitable for both interior and exterior applications. Surface light structures are single piece, seamless parts as thin as 7mm as compared to 25+mm required for conventional electronics. Marketed B2B to OEMs and Tier suppliers, our unique technology licensing business model fosters a collaborative ecosystem, advancing high-performance, user-centric designs with IMSE® (Injection Molded Structural Electronics) technology.

# KATR

## Basic Information
- Company: Kubota North America
- Honor: 2025 Best of Innovation in Industrial Equipment and Machinery
- Categories: Industrial Equipment and Machinery
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/katr/

![KATR](https://www.ces.tech/media/zaenq2ot/katr.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The KATR is a four-wheeled robot designed to provide a stable platform on uneven terrain. It features a unique stability control system that adjusts the robot's four legs to maintain a level cargo deck, even on hills and slopes. Powered by either combustion engine or electric drive, the robot has a load capacity of 240 kg and can be controlled either remotely or via an onboard controller. The KATR is compact, yet robust enough for off-road applications in agriculture and construction. It is the first of its kind to be practically applied in such demanding environments.

- Categories: Computer Peripherals & Accessories
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/keychron-k2-he-wireless-magnetic-custom-keyboard/

![Keychron K2 HE Wireless Magnetic Custom Keyboard](https://www.ces.tech/media/irib5mqc/keychronk2hewirelessmagneticcustomkeyboard.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The Keychron K2 HE redefines mechanical keyboards with magnetic switches, offering customizable actuation points from 0.2-3.8mm with 0.1mm precision. It can program and customize the key's trigger distance and triggered value, allowing users to program each key's function and assign varied actions to a single key depending on how deeply it is pressed. It gives users unlimited possibilities. This 75% layout keyboard supports wired and wireless (2.4GHz, Bluetooth) connectivity. It features a premium design with natural wood finishes and RGB backlightings. The K2 HE has a web-based configurator, which makes it compatible with Windows, macOS, Android, and even Linux.

# LCD Sun-Burn Free Conventional AR HUD

## Basic Information
- Company: Hyundai Mobis
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Vehicle Tech & Advanced Mobility
- Categories: Vehicle Tech & Advanced Mobility
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/lcd-sun-burn-free-conventional-ar-hud/

![LCD Sun-Burn Free Conventional AR HUD](https://www.ces.tech/media/tcdjlzad/lcdsun-burnfreeconventionalarhud.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
AR-HUD should have a wide FoV to show AR information. However, for AR-HUD with a wide FoV range, it is difficult to use LCD-based PGUs, because a lot of solar energy is concentrated on the PGU and cause damage. Therefore, most AR-HUDs are based on DLP/LCoS projection PGUs, which are expensive and show the same or lower image quality. This problem is a big problem for expanding the AR-HUD market. MOBIS has developed a sun-burn issue for LCD-based PGUs, which has price competitiveness and good image quality, so we believe that it will greatly contribute to expanding the AR market.

## Basic Information
- Company: HHS Co.,Ltd.

## Description
HHS developed an intelligent IoT system that combines bio-signal processing technology and complex sensing technology in order to analyze and monitor workers' individual risk status and health in real time for the four most common accident types (fall, bump, suffocation, and heat-related illness) that occur in ultra-high-risk workplaces. This system provides a data-based integrated worker safety management service that determines risks through analysis of workers' individual movement patterns and EEG analysis technology and combines harmful gas detection technology using IoT sensor arrays.

# LPDDR5X 10.7Gbps

## Basic Information
- Company: Samsung Electronics America, Inc.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Mobile Devices, Accessories & Apps
- Categories: Mobile Devices, Accessories & Apps
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/lpddr5x-107gbps/

![LPDDR5X 10.7Gbps](https://www.ces.tech/media/boxnsijl/lpddr5x107gbps.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Samsung Electronics has developed the industry's first LPDDR5X DRAM, achieving speeds of up to 10.7 Gbps using 12 nanometer-class process technology. This development advances the performance of low-power DRAM and is the smallest chip size among existing LPDDRs. The technology is designed to support the increasing requirements of AI-driven applications from PCs, servers, and vehicles to emerging on-device AI applications, offering a balance of high performance and energy efficiency. LPDDR5X solidifies Samsung's position in the low-power DRAM memory market.

- Categories: Artificial Intelligence
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/luci/

![LUCI](https://www.ces.tech/media/aqqdtaec/luci.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
LUCI is a privacy-first, temporal computing platform designed to bring lifelong memory and context-aware intelligence to your fingertips. At its core is a custom operating system, Life OS, which enables intuitive, on-demand recall of life events through a highly personalized AI assistant, Contextual Intelligence. This assistant operates with a comprehensive understanding of the user's life context, powered by our proprietary Memory-augmented video intelligence (Mavi).Components:1. The Pin: A wearable and interactable intelligence pin featuring a high-definition 12MP ultra-wide lens and dual microphones, capable of capturing over 4 hours of continuous video and audio. It includes a privacy switch, allowing users to quickly disable the camera and microphones, giving them complete control over personal data capture at any time.2. The Hub: This unit serves as the processing center, housing the AI's ""brain."" The Hub stores and processes data locally, sharing the user's memories only with their Contextual Intelligence assistant. With privacy as a top priority, no data is uploaded to the cloud without explicit user consent, keeping all computations and memory storage entirely local.

# MCE’s Styrofoam Upcycling and Sustainable Agriculture

## Basic Information
- Company: MCE Inc.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Food & AgTech
- Categories: Food & AgTech
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/mce-s-styrofoam-upcycling-and-sustainable-agriculture/

![MCE’s Styrofoam Upcycling and Sustainable Agriculture](https://www.ces.tech/media/vrwbwpis/matter-compliantwirelessly-poweredsmarthomeautomationsensors.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
MCE provides a container module that processes styrofoam into feed blocks, enabling mealworms to break it down effectively. This module is easily installed and expanded, making it an efficient solution for styrofoam waste. MCE's process reduces carbon emissions by 93% compared to recycling and over 99% compared to incineration, minimizing environmental impact. The UNEP warns that styrofoam's social costs could reach $25 billion by 2025, highlighting the need for such solutions. MCE's feed blocks allow mealworms to consume up to 92% of styrofoam and convert it into organic fertilizer in just one day, supporting sustainable agriculture and global food security.

# MEW air purifier

## Description

Compact and portable, it fits easily into vehicle cup holders, making it ideal for personal use in various environments. Its unique design eliminates the need for filters, offering a maintenance-free and eco-friendly solution for air purification.

# Mobile Ankle-foot Exoneuromusculoskeleton

## Basic Information
- Company: The Hong Kong Polytechnic University
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Accessibility & AgeTech
- Categories: Accessibility & AgeTech
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/mobile-ankle-foot-exoneuromusculoskeleton/

![Mobile Ankle-foot Exoneuromusculoskeleton](https://www.ces.tech/media/ysajcu1d/mobileankle-footexoneuromusculoskeleton.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The mobile ankle-foot exoneuromusculoskeleton (ENMS) is the first-of-its-kind that integrates multi-modal advantages of exoskeletons, soft pneumatic muscles, neuromuscular electrical stimulation (NMES), and vibrotactile sensory feedback into a single, lightweight wearable system powered by a 9V rechargeable battery. This unique combination not only allows for effective correction of post-stroke footdrop and foot inversion, which are common issues faced by stroke patients, but also makes the whole system easy to use by non-professionals in self-help telerehabilitation.

# MOGLU: Noninvasive Continuous Glucose Monitoring Device

## Basic Information
- Company: Apollon
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Digital Health
- Categories: Digital Health
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/moglu-noninvasive-continuous-glucose-monitoring-device/

![MOGLU: Noninvasive Continuous Glucose Monitoring Device](https://www.ces.tech/media/uwmoep4u/moglu.png?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
MOGLU is a noninvasive continuous glucose monitoring (CGM) device designed to revolutionize diabetes care. Using innovative Raman spectroscopy technology, it detects glucose-reactive signals on the skin, reducing costs and enhancing convenience. We are the only team worldwide to directly observe in vivo Raman signals for glucose. Since 2023, we've collaborated with Professor Peter So's team at MIT's Biological Engineering department on clinical trials. We plan to conduct larger trials at the Joslin Diabetes Center later this year and aim for FDA approval in 2025. Our data so far indicates that MOGLU could potentially become the first FDA-approved noninvasive CGM.


---

# molluSCAN 2.0

## Basic Information
- Company: molluSCAN-eye
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Sustainability & Energy/Power
- Categories: Sustainability & Energy/Power
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/molluscan-20/

![molluSCAN 2.0](https://www.ces.tech/media/11ep3oj5/molluscan-20.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
molluSCAN provides a bio-monitoring system that harnesses the natural sensitivity of bivalve mollusks to assess water quality continuously. This technology combines electronics, mathematics, and biology to provide 24/7 monitoring of aquatic environments. By equipping oysters, mussels, or other bivalves with non-invasive sensors, the system tracks their behavior, including valve movements and stress responses, as indicators of water pollution. The mollusks act as living sentinels, offering early warning detection of contaminants and environmental changes. This solution enables industries, municipalities and environmental agencies to monitor water quality in real-time, enhancing their ability to protect aquatic ecosystems and respond swiftly to pollution events.


---

![Motion Wi-Fi Sensing Plug](https://www.ces.tech/media/odwcudhe/motionwi-fisensingplug.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Threshold’s Motion Wi-Fi Sensing Plug (Motion) is the first-of-its-kind, non-invasive Wi-Fi sensing smart plug designed to provide real-time motion insights to caregivers and family members without using cameras or wearables. Motion is a simple and easy-to-use solution that provides family caregivers insights into motion patterns for an overall understanding of the well-being of their loved ones, all without requiring any behavior changes from those being provided care.

# MouthPad^

## Basic Information
- Company: Augmental
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Accessibility & AgeTech
- Categories: Accessibility & AgeTech
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/mouthpad/

![MouthPad^](https://www.ces.tech/media/vb4f3viz/untitled-9.png?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
At Augmental, we redesigned the computer mouse from the ground up to make it more universally accessible. The MouthPad^ is an intraoral interface that enables hands-free control of digital devices — including computers, tablets and smartphones — using tongue and head gestures. It offers seamless Bluetooth connectivity and is compatible with all common operating systems as a wireless mouse. Custom-fitted for comfort and made with dental-grade materials, the MouthPad^ is designed to enhance accessibility for users with disabilities and provide intuitive, mouth-based interaction for all.

# Multi-Mic+

## Basic Information
- Company: GN Group
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Accessibility & AgeTech
- Categories: Accessibility & AgeTech
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/multi-micplus/

![Multi-Mic+](https://www.ces.tech/media/ki2drogp/caf724f8-6a5f-488a-bd6e-119856611849.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The Multi-Mic+ is a wireless remote microphone designed to enhance hearing experiences in challenging listening environments. As well as supporting Telecoil, FM systems, and DAI/direct audio input, it’s the world’s first remote microphone with Bluetooth® Low Energy (LE) Audio and AuracastTM broadcast audio technology, revolutionizing wireless connectivity. Unlike traditional remote microphones which are limited to specific hearing aid brands, the Multi-Mic+ can broadcast audio to multiple users simultaneously, regardless of their device type. This includes hearing aids, cochlear implants, earbuds or any other Auracast enabled device, making it the most inclusive solution for diverse needs.

# Nano-Stream

## Description
Nano-Stream is the industry’s most efficient automated storage and retrieval system (AS/RS), designed for unparalleled flexibility and scalability. Unlike conventional systems that are designed for at least 10,000 square feet, Nano-Stream can be effectively installed in spaces as small as 1,000 square feet, achieving high storage density and transport capacity. It utilizes demountable cranes and AGVs for product retrieval, allowing for easy initial installation with potential for scaling. This significant reduction in labor costs and space requirements positions our solution uniquely in the untapped niche of warehouse automation.

Industrials send their targeted biochemicals to our laboratories, along with an online questionnaire on the mode of action of the compound and how it is supposed to affect crop growth, preservation or processing. After one week, the app will provide predictive data on potential toxicology effects that could impact human health with the risk of developing associated diseases.

# Novel Flash LiDAR  with SiPM Sensor and Diffraction Optics

## Basic Information
- Company: Integrated Quantum Photonics Inc. (IQP)
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Vehicle Tech & Advanced Mobility
- Categories: Vehicle Tech & Advanced Mobility
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/novel-flash-lidar-with-sipm-sensor-and-diffraction-optics/

![Novel Flash LiDAR  with SiPM Sensor and Diffraction Optics](https://www.ces.tech/media/m1gpdp13/28f8ef21-6f28-41f7-a752-20b61c99758d.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The Flash LiDAR is a technology designed to enhance the capabilities of high-level autonomous driving. This system operates on the Flash Mode of Light Detection and Ranging (LiDAR) using the Time-of-Flight (ToF) method. The Flash Mode is enabled by Diffraction Optics, which distributes the laser beam across the field of view with a flexible scanning rate up to the kHz range. The integration of a CMOS-based microSiPM Optical Sensor ensures high sensitivity and provides 3D camera imagery, including ranging information, with intelligent on-chip processing. The system's compact design and modular structure make it versatile for various automotive applications.

## Description

Pawport connects via WiFi to the Pawport app, enabling remote control and management, curfew and other scheduling functionality, voice control via Alexa, Siri, or Google, and pet-specific tracking and usage data. Pets utilize the door by virtue of a small, lightweight, waterproof Bluetooth collar tag that verifies the pet and opens Pawport when the pet is near.

## Basic Information
- Company: Gbrain

- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/phin-stim-wireless-brain-monitorstimulation-implant/

## Description
Phin Stim, developed by Gbrain, is a groundbreaking wireless neural implant redefining care for neurological conditions like Parkinson’s and epilepsy. Leveraging real-time brainwave monitoring and advanced therapeutic stimulation, Phin Stim delivers personalized treatment directly at the brain cortex without scalp-attached wires or invasive deep-brain penetration. Its innovative thin-film polymer electrode ensures superior flexibility and minimal tissue impact, offering precision, safety, and comfort. Designed for portability, Phin Stim enables on-the-go neuroplasticity therapy, empowering patients to maintain active lives while receiving continuous care.

# PRiMX50U-Power

## Basic Information
- Company: SAMSUNG SDI
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Industrial Equipment and Machinery
- Categories: Industrial Equipment and Machinery
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/primx50u-power/

![PRiMX50U-Power](https://www.ces.tech/media/zpwj133y/primx50u-power.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
PRiMX50U-Power is the world's most powerful 21700-sized cylindrical 5.0Ah battery, driving the expansion of cordless products with advanced Tab-less technology. This innovative technology enhances alignment control, improves safety, and reduces resistance by 20% due to the thinner electrode plate that supports high power performance. The 5.0Ah capacity is achieved with 91% high-nickel cathode material and SCN(Si-Carbon-Nanocomposite) anode material. PRiMX50U-Power can charge to 80% capacity in just 15 minutes and provides more than three years of use without degradation. *PRiMX stands for "Prime Battery for Maximum Experience" which is SAMSUNG SDI's battery brand that encompasses all of our technologies and innovations.

# PRiMX680-EV

## Basic Information
- Company: SAMSUNG SDI
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Sustainability & Energy/Power
- Categories: Sustainability & Energy/Power
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/primx680-ev/

![PRiMX680-EV](https://www.ces.tech/media/q1hf5jua/primx680-ev.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
PRiMX680-EV cell is SAMSUNG SDI's most up-to-date battery cell for electric vehicles with a capacity of 178Ah, standing as the world’s highest-capacity prismatic NCM cell. By utilizing cutting-edge high-nickel NCA materials and a sophisticated stacking process, it delivers an exceptional 680Wh/L energy density. This ensures significantly extended driving ranges, a crucial factor in meeting the growing demands of modern electric vehicle (EV) consumers. The cell’s robust prismatic design is engineered with top terminals and innovative directional venting, effectively managing gas flow in the unlikely event of a failure, thereby enhancing overall safety and reliability. *PRiMX is SAMSUNG SDI's battery brand.


---

# PRiMX680 Module+

## Basic Information
- Company: SAMSUNG SDI
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Sustainability & Energy/Power
- Categories: Sustainability & Energy/Power
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/primx680-moduleplus/

## Description
PRiMX680 Module+, our advanced EV battery module, integrates SAMSUNG SDI's 178Ah high-capacity prismatic NCM cells, delivering industry-leading energy efficiency and significantly extending driving ranges. It incorporates cutting-edge wireless CSC(Cell Sensor Circuit) technology, enhancing production efficiency and reliability by simplifying the module’s internal design. The module is versatile and suitable for a wide range of EV applications, from compact city cars to larger, more demanding vehicles, making it a pivotal component in the rapidly evolving automotive market. The integration of the thinner 131Ah cell variant further offers even greater flexibility for various vehicle configurations. *PRiMX is SAMSUNG SDI's battery brand.

# ProPury

## Basic Information
- Company: Inc. ENGITEIN
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Sustainability & Energy/Power
- Categories: Sustainability & Energy/Power
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/propury/

![ProPury](https://www.ces.tech/media/koujkcfl/a52e6bb5-7978-4221-b0b4-a7cd201dd27f.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Our eco-friendly antibody purification device, ProPury revolutionizes biotechnology by enabling rapid, efficient antibody production from animal cells. Utilizing the innovative ENGI-R reagent, antibodies are enlarged and separated from the culture medium through a specialized capture filter, powered by our device's pump. Harvested with ENGI-EL reagent, the antibodies are ready for diverse research applications. By eliminating the need for Protein A resins and organic solvents, this technology is not only economical but also environmentally responsible. It significantly enhances researchers' productivity, reducing both time and costs in antibody production.

# SAI-VDS: Victim Detection System with Reflection Control (Surveillance Camera System)

## Basic Information
- Company: Sai Technologies Co., Ltd.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Human Security for All
- Categories: Human Security for All
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/sai-vds-victim-detection-system-with-reflection-control-surveillance-camera-system/

![SAI-VDS: Victim Detection System with Reflection Control (Surveillance Camera System)](https://www.ces.tech/media/yccnd2eg/101322327_sai-vds-1.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The Victim Detection System (VDS) integrates automatic reflection control into surveillance cameras to capture optimal images and enhance AI recognition. One of the most crucial factors in rescuing victims is the time it takes to locate them. However, surfaces like water and snow are highly reflective, making detection difficult. VDS addresses this issue by combining reflection control cameras with AI analysis.This technology is compatible with any camera, including single-camera systems, regardless of the manufacturer. For existing video surveillance systems, it can be easily implemented by simply replacing the cameras. It enables precise control of the light entering the lens or the human eye, allowing versatile applications in devices like smartphones, sunglasses, binoculars and scopes.

# SBB1.5

- Company: SAMSUNG SDI
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Sustainability & Energy/Power
- Categories: Sustainability & Energy/Power

These features not only enhance system performance but also reduce total cost of ownership (TCO), ensuring stable operation of the ESS system and maximizing customer profitability.

# SBMS for Lithium Battery Fire Extinguishment

## Basic Information
- Company: KOREA LFP
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Sustainability & Energy/Power
- Categories: Sustainability & Energy/Power
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/sbms-for-lithium-battery-fire-extinguishment/

![SBMS for Lithium Battery Fire Extinguishment](https://www.ces.tech/media/gvqdwhqg/dafd2735-6bb1-4f21-a5f8-0b3f0b2696cd.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The SBMS(Smart safe Battery Management System) we developed is the world's first product to integrate a fire extinguishing device, a smart safety feature, into the existing battery management system (BMS). Installed in battery packs for electric vehicles, ESS, and e-mobility using lithium batteries, it offers more than just overcharge and overdischarge protection and cell balancing. SBMS continuously monitors battery cell temperatures, and if abnormal heat is detected, it automatically releases CO2 to cool the cells and remove oxygen within the module. This effectively prevents thermal runaway and extinguishes fires, significantly enhancing the protection of human life and societal safety.

# Self-Contained Power Supply Coin Battery

## Basic Information
- Company: SMK Electronics Corp.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Sustainability & Energy/Power
- Categories: Sustainability & Energy/Power
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/self-contained-power-supply-coin-battery/

![Self-Contained Power Supply Coin Battery](https://www.ces.tech/media/5c2fokip/self-containedpowersupplycoinbattery.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The self-contained power supply (SCPS) coin battery consists of a high efficiency solar panel and a power storage device all within the dimensions of a CR2032 coin cell battery. When used in battery powered devices that are exposed to ambient light, this SCPS coin battery charges itself, ensuring that you have power when you need it. The SCPS coin battery also has an RF radio to monitor its charge level along with sensors to measure acceleration, temperature and humidity. It is designed to fit into battery compartments that work with CR2032 cells without modifications.

## Basic Information
- Company: Myant Corp.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Digital Health
- Categories: Digital Health
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/skiin-cardiac-monitoring-smart-garments/

## Description
Electrocardiographs (ECG) are the cornerstone of cardiac diagnostics and monitoring, however, the base technology behind ECG to-date has lacked innovation. We have developed the first textile-based clinical-grade ECG monitoring platform. Our platform has been engineered to allow patients to start their care journey via a traditional 24-hour to 14-day Holter study, and seamlessly transition into a long-term monitoring program. This first-of-its-kind comprehensive cardiac monitoring solution includes Holter monitoring, continuous ECG, blood pressure, glucose, weight, SpO2, and temperature. With a machine learning based arrhythmia monitoring system, complex cardiac disorders can be identified earlier and managed more aggressively.

# Smart Self-cleaning Air Purifier

## Basic Information
- Company: COWAY
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Sustainability & Energy/Power
- Categories: Sustainability & Energy/Power
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/smart-self-cleaning-air-purifier/

![Smart Self-cleaning Air Purifier](https://www.ces.tech/media/uh4fygwx/smartself-cleaningairpurifier.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
This device is an air purifier developed to tackle the inconvenience of cleaning and replacing filters. It examines the device usage to calculate the appropriate cycle for cleaning, spraying steam and water on the filter to clean it. Once the cleaning is done, it notifies the user to empty the water tank via the mobile app or directly through the device. In addition, it analyzes the outdoor and indoor air quality to provide the right purifying mode for the current indoor air quality. These functions allow for efficient use of energy and enhance the user experience.

# SWEAR Security

## Basic Information
- Company: Swear
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Human Security for All
- Categories: Human Security for All
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/swear-security/

![SWEAR Security](https://www.ces.tech/media/1cpmltkq/swearsecurity.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
SWEAR’s patented technology captures and protects digital content at the point of creation. This means every frame of a video, every sound bite, and every pixel is immediately secured with a unique cryptographic fingerprint (Digital DNA) and written into a blockchain ledger. Unlike traditional forensic methods that reactively work to identify fakes, SWEAR authenticates every piece of digital content from the start, ensuring a continuous chain of custody that cannot be tampered with.

# Three-Axis Micro Gimbal Stabilizer

## Basic Information
- Company: Vista Innotech Limited
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Imaging
- Categories: Imaging
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/three-axis-micro-gimbal-stabilizer/

![Three-Axis Micro Gimbal Stabilizer](https://www.ces.tech/media/1phbsfbt/three-axismicrogimbalstabilizer.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The 3-axis Micro Gimbal Stabilizer (MGS) is the world's smallest 3-axis gimbal camera with up to ±8° compensation angle . The MGS is a patented motor structure consisting of only 4 ball bearings, which is much less than at least 12 ball bearings in the traditional 3-axis gimbal. The MGS can be embedded into various mobile devices, extending the exposure time by 16 times and enabling mobile devices to capture clear images even in low light and extreme conditions. With the latest 5G technology, our MGS enables sharp and smooth video live streaming for life-critical applications.

# V2G AC home EV charger supporting AMI-based VPP solution

## Basic Information
- Company: Motrex
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Sustainability & Energy/Power, Smart Home
- Categories: Sustainability & Energy/Power, Smart Home
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/v2g-ac-home-ev-charger-supporting-ami-based-vpp-solution/

![V2G AC home EV charger supporting AMI-based VPP solution](https://www.ces.tech/media/5sgls25t/v2g-ac-home-ev-charger-supporting-ami-based-vpp-solution.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Integrating V2G (Vehicle-to-Grid) Technology with VPP (Virtual Power Plant) in Smart Homes: This solution transforms electric vehicles (EVs) into integral components of the smart home ecosystem, enabling them to not only serve as transportation but also as energy storage units. By integrating with a VPP, EVs can interact seamlessly with home energy systems, optimizing electricity usage and providing backup power during peak times. Advanced technologies like AMI (Advanced Metering Infrastructure), DCU (Data Concentration Unit), and HES (Head-End System) make it possible for households to manage energy efficiently and participate in the energy market.

# VET CAI

## Basic Information
- Company: BrainU Co., Ltd.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Pet Tech & Animal Welfare
- Categories: Pet Tech & Animal Welfare
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/vet-cai/

![VET CAI](https://www.ces.tech/media/b4lmtoea/vetcai.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
VET CAI is the world's first EEG-based anesthesia depth meter developed exclusively for animals that tracks the level of consciousness during surgery and monitors the depth of anesthesia by indexing it. This helps prevent deaths from over-anesthesia or traumatic awakening during medical procedures. The main advantages over traditional EEG measurement methods are that it does not hurt the body (non-invasive), does not remove hair, and can safely monitor anesthesia in real time.

# VIB Energy Tile: Specialized Indoor Energy Storage

## Basic Information
- Company: Standard Energy
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Smart Cities
- Categories: Smart Cities
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/vib-energy-tile-specialized-indoor-energy-storage/

![VIB Energy Tile: Specialized Indoor Energy Storage](https://www.ces.tech/media/gbsgfp1u/vibenergytilespecializedindoorenergystorage.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The VIB Energy Tile is a pioneering energy storage system (ESS) built with the world’s first vanadium-ion battery, specifically designed for energy storage applications. Its advanced technology ensures exceptional longevity, achieving over 100,000 charge-discharge cycles, ten times more than other commercial batteries. The water-based, low heat mechanism minimizes fire and explosion risks, even during external fires. With a focus on eco-friendliness, the product’s simple design enables efficient manufacturing, easy disassembly, and high energy efficiency, making it a sustainable solution throughout its entire lifecycle.

# Voice to Braille

## Basic Information
- Company: SignTech
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Accessibility & AgeTech
- Categories: Accessibility & AgeTech
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/voice-to-braille/

![Voice to Braille](https://www.ces.tech/media/jgmfld0d/voicetobraille-1.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Voice to Braille is a device that instantly converts spoken voice into Braille, allowing the 93% of visually impaired individuals who cannot read or write Braille to easily create, edit, and print Braille text without any additional training.Voice to Braille features a precise microphone system for accurate voice recognition and advanced AI that converts speech into both digital text and Braille data. The Braille data can be freely edited and output as audio through the device's hyper-directional speaker or transferred to other devices, including Braille printers, enhancing accessibility and seamless communication.

# Watatumi: AI-powered Smart Fish Farm Software Suite

## Basic Information
- Company: Aizip & Softbank Corp.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Food & AgTech
- Categories: Food & AgTech
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/watatumi-ai-powered-smart-fish-farm-software-suite/

![Watatumi: AI-powered Smart Fish Farm Software Suite](https://www.ces.tech/media/3qnjq35f/watatumi-ai-powered-smart-fish-farm-monitoring.png?rxy=0.4974937343358396,0.5350877192982456&width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Watatumi is an AI-powered software suite for monitoring critical fish farming activities, including feeding, cage monitoring, and fish transferring. It features deep neural network models for fish counting, fishnet damage detection, and fish size estimation. These models, powered by innovative efficient neural network architectures, deployed on embedded chipsets near underwater cameras, eliminating the need to transmit large video data out of water, improving reliability, reducing costs, and simplifying integration. The algorithms consistently achieve high accuracy under varying  lighting, water, and weather conditions, and adapt easily to different camera setups. Watatumi significantly improves the efficiency and profitability of fish farming.
