# XanderGlasses Connect

## Basic Information
- Company: Xander
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Accessibility & AgeTech
- Categories: Accessibility & AgeTech
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/xanderglasses-connect/

![XanderGlasses Connect](https://www.ces.tech/media/nl1ed2ls/xanderglassesconnect.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
XanderGlasses Connect is wearable assistive technology designed to help people who struggle to hear or understand speech. Our first product, XanderGlasses, translates speech to text in real-time and projects accurate captions for the wearer. Our new product XG Connect adds functionality and features: AI text transformers to help wearers with cognitive challenges, captioning of environmental sounds (not just speech), 26 languages, cloud-based translation between languages, and a smartphone app for personalization. XanderGlasses Connect allows wearers to capture and store conversations which is helpful for seniors who want to record a medical or legal appointment to share information with family.


---

# xMEMS µCooling

## Basic Information
- Company: xMEMS Labs, Inc.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Computer Hardware & Components
- Categories: Computer Hardware & Components
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/xmems-%C2%B5cooling/

![xMEMS µCooling](https://www.ces.tech/media/1mnht5jb/xmemscooling.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
xMEMS µCooling (part number XMC-2400) is the first all-silicon fan-on-a-chip bringing active cooling to thin, AI-enabled mobile electronics. The 1mm-thin cooling chip generates airflow to actively cool devices such as smartphones, tablets, laptops, wireless chargers and SSD which are typically only passively cooled today.


---

# XoMotion™

## Basic Information
- Company: Human In Motion Robotics Inc.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Robotics
- Categories: Robotics
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/xomotion/

![XoMotion™](https://www.ces.tech/media/sc1npusu/xomotion.png?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
XoMotion™ is the world’s most advanced wearable robotic exoskeleton, designed to assist patients with mobility impairments due to spinal cord injuries, stroke, and other neurological conditions in standing up and walking. This lower-limb medical device offers unparalleled multi-directional locomotion support through self-balancing and hands-free functionality, enabling customizable and task-oriented robotic rehabilitation treatments across various stages of recovery. XoMotion™ not only enhances patient outcomes but also reduces cognitive load and physical strain on therapists in rehabilitation clinics. The technology has recently received Health Canada approval for sales in Canada and is currently undergoing clinical trials in the US for FDA approval.


---

# XPG LANCER NEON

## Basic Information
- Company: ADATA Technology Co., Ltd.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Computer Hardware & Components
- Categories: Computer Hardware & Components
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/xpg-lancer-neon/

![XPG LANCER NEON](https://www.ces.tech/media/ii1cbvcw/xpglancerneon.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The XPG LANCER NEON DDR5 memory module is the world's first environmentally friendly RGB gaming memory module. It features an industry leading 60% illuminated RGB area and is made of 50% eco-friendly PCR materials, reducing carbon emissions by 72.5%. An IMR process further reduces environmental impact. This product also features an exclusive PCB heat dissipating coating that reduces heat by 10%.

# XREAL One and XREAL One Pro

## Basic Information
- Company: XREAL
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in XR Technologies & Accessories
- Categories: XR Technologies & Accessories
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/xreal-one-and-xreal-one-pro/

![XREAL One and XREAL One Pro](https://www.ces.tech/media/4poowyzr/xrealoneandxrealonepro.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
XREAL One and XREAL One Pro build on the success of the XREAL Air series, the world’s best selling AR glasses, giving consumers access to a next-gen spatial computing experience, adding a never-before-seen custom design using a built-in processor that offers a low latency 3DoF spatial screen experience regardless of source device. Giving users a massive screen with a FOV of up to 57-degrees, universal 120Hz refresh rate, an improved spatial speaker system from BOSE, and adjustable Inter Pupillary Distance ranges, XREAL One and XREAL One Pro also debut a unique RGB modular camera with multimodal AI support.

# Yaber Ultra Short Throw Laser Projector K300s

## Basic Information
- Company: Yaber Technologies Co., Limited
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Content & Entertainment
- Categories: Content & Entertainment
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/yaber-ultra-short-throw-laser-projector-k300s/

![Yaber Ultra Short Throw Laser Projector K300s](https://www.ces.tech/media/zvgdrbqn/yaberultrashortthrowlaserprojectork300s.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Yaber Ultra Short Throw Laser Projector K300s combines cutting-edge technology to seamlessly integrate high-end projector into modern home living. Its leading Ultra Short Throw(UST) optical technology and JBL audio system deliver an unparalleled large-screen experience for home theaters. The ultra-high 950lm ensures clear, vibrant visuals even in daylight or well-lit environments, while the automatic focus and intelligent eye protection design enhance viewing comfort, creating an immersive audiovisual feast.

# Yarbo

## Basic Information
- Company: Shenzhen Hanyang Technology Co., Ltd.
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Robotics
- Categories: Robotics
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/yarbo/

![Yarbo](https://www.ces.tech/media/h4ublpox/yarbo.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Yarbo (2024 Model) is an innovative modular robot designed to autonomously maintain yards and outdoor spaces year-round. Yarbo supports a modular design, enabling a variety of tasks such as mowing, leaf blowing and snow blowing, customizing to different weather conditions and maintenance needs. Leveraging AI and RTK-GPS technology, Yarbo navigates and operates independently with impeccable precision. Each unit can be controlled through a mobile device app, offering a convenient and customized user experience. The robot’s design prioritizes sustainability and is user-friendly, making Yarbo a competitive alternative to traditional lawn maintenance.

# YLM-10LX 3D LiDAR sensor

## Basic Information
- Company: Lumotive and Hokuyo
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Robotics
- Categories: Robotics
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/ylm-10lx-3d-lidar-sensor/

![YLM-10LX 3D LiDAR sensor](https://www.ces.tech/media/0irn0mgx/e473094a-5dad-45fe-8902-7e591052c6c8.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
The Hokuyo YLM-10LX is a state-of-the-art solid-state 3D LiDAR sensor tailored for industrial automation and service robotics. Created by Hokuyo, a prominent name in the LiDAR industry, it incorporates Lumotive's pioneering Light Control Metasurface (LCM™) technology, representing the forefront of programmable optics. This sensor delivers outstanding range, field of view, and reliability, all achieved without moving components. The YLM-10LX boasts precise, programmable scanning capabilities, ensuring reliable performance in dynamic settings. Its compact form and advanced optical beam steering make it the perfect option for applications that require top-notch 3D sensing and obstacle detection.

# Z890 AORUS XTREME AI TOP

- Company: GIGABYTE Technology
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Artificial Intelligence
- Categories: Artificial Intelligence
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/z890-aorus-xtreme-ai-top/

## Description
Built with superior power design, multi-GPU support, the flagship Z890 AORUS XTREME AI TOP motherboard can release the ultimate performance of the latest gen processor for gaming, overclocking, and local AI training. With exclusive AI TOP Utility, it can optimize AI training and fine-tuning while maintaining privacy and security. Featuring next-gen connectivity of WIFI7, dual 10GbE LAN, and the latest Thunderbolt 5 brings blistering network and connection, while the  DTS:X® Ultra audio creates an immersive gaming experience for gamers. DIY-friendly advancements like AORUS AI SNATCH, EZ-Debug Zone, WIFI EZ-Plug, EZ-Latch, and UC BIOS create friendly system building experience for users.

# Zeos Audiva

## Basic Information
- Company: Zeos Global
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Mobile Devices, Accessories & Apps
- Categories: Mobile Devices, Accessories & Apps
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/zeos-audiva/

![Zeos Audiva](https://www.ces.tech/media/p41dbud3/zeosaudiva.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
Zeos Audiva is the world’s first noise-cancelling directional microphone attachment for smartphones, featuring real-time noise-canceling technology for transmitting crystal clear audio in any environment. Plugs directly into your device’s type-C port – no Bluetooth required. Audiva is ideal for phone calls – both regular and speaker-phone, professional recordings, field reporting and virtual meetings. Its fixed mic-to-sound-source distance ensures optimal performance, eliminating virtually all noise that's over 9-12 inches away from the device. Sleek, portable and user-friendly, Audiva is designed to enhance the user’s audio experience – even in extremely noisy areas. It is compatible with Androids and iPhone 15/16 series,

# [SL-2.2] High-Resolution SPAD Sensor for LiDAR

## Basic Information
- Company: SolidVue
- Honor: 2025 Honoree in Smart Cities
- Categories: Smart Cities
- URL: https://www.ces.tech/ces-innovation-awards/2025/sl-22-high-resolution-spad-sensor-for-lidar/

![[SL-2.2] High-Resolution SPAD Sensor for LiDAR](https://www.ces.tech/media/oeyj3wuf/sl-22-high-resolution-spad-sensor-new-image.jpg?width=1000&height=666&format=webp&quality=80)

## Description
SolidVUE will showcase its SL-2.2 at CES 2025—the world’s first 400x128 high-resolution single-chip LiDAR sensor IC designed for compact solid-state LiDAR. Paired with a VCSEL array-based emitter, this technology offers lower cost, smaller size, and improved vibration reliability compared to traditional mechanical LiDAR. The SL-2.2 integrates a high-density SPAD pixel array, time-to-digital converter (TDC), image signal processor, and peripheral circuits on a single chip. It delivers 400x128 high-resolution 3D point-cloud images with a wide Field-of-View (FOV), enabling precise object detection up to 200 meters, making it ideal for autonomous vehicles, security, and robotics applications.
